msg:I recently had the pleasure of staying at an amazing hotel and I must say, it exceeded all my expectations. One of the highlights of my stay was the delicious breakfast. The hotel offered a wide variety of options, from fresh fruit to hot dishes, and everything was prepared to perfection. 

Another great feature of this hotel was the big outdoor swimming pool. My kids absolutely loved it! The pool was not only spacious, but it was also designed with children in mind, making it safe and enjoyable for kids of all ages. It was the perfect way for my family to cool off and have some fun in the sun.

One thing that stood out to me about this hotel was its cleanliness. The rooms were spotless, and the common areas were always well-maintained. It was clear that the hotel took great pride in providing a clean and comfortable environment for its guests.

Lastly, I was pleasantly surprised to find out that the hotel allowed for late check-out. This meant that we could take our time in the morning and didn't have to rush to leave. It was a small gesture, but it made a big difference in our overall experience.

Overall, I highly recommend this hotel. The good breakfast, kid-friendly swimming pool, cleanliness, and accommodating late check-out policy all contributed to a wonderful stay. I can't wait to visit again!

name:P‚ÄçB‚ÄçS‚ÄçH‚ÄçE‚ÄçL‚ÄçE‚ÄçY
info:Deluxe Premier King Bed Room
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Other
info:2 Reviews

posted:Posted October 4, 2021
msg:I stayed at the Langham Shenzhen for two nights. I chose the hotel because the hotel has a light, bright, classic feel to it. I was not disappointed, the hotel has a very nice blend of classic hotel style and modern convenience. The hotel was absolutely clean and well cared for; the entrance, lobbies, elevators, restaurants, pool and spa were wonderful. The hotel feels refreshing in a subdued manner- not like the overpowering sensation of scent one feels upon entering some of today's trendy hotels. The Langham is also not trying to be trendy, it's simply an exquisitely appointed comfort zone that provides guests a sumptuous, refreshing place to relax and enjoy themselves. The staff is utterly professional and helpful; there is no sense of pretentiousness, simply a sense of desire to provide the best service possible. 

Upon entering my room, the drapes opened and the television turned on to classical music. The room was stunningly appointed and very comfortable. I haven't slept so well in years- even while staying at some famous five-star hotels. I visited two of the hotels restaurants, but as this was a relaxing weekend staycation, I ordered room service the entire time. Again, the staff was beyond professional and helpful, they listened to me practice my Mandarin and tried to understand me, but they were always willing to speak English when I couldn't express my thoughts in Mandarin. The food was well presented and for the most part tasted good. Their eggs were a bit overcooked, but that is the only thing I can complain about. The spa was very clean and comfortable. It is not inexpensive, but I felt so cared for and so comfortable (even now- days later) that I plan to come back in the future. 

The Langham is a wonderful hotel to stay at. It exceeds in all the ways a hotel should- cleanliness, luxurious appointments, comfort and helpful, professional service. Why stay anywhere else? 4.7/5.0
----------------------------------------

Stay in the executive room and get free afternoon tea for two and evening cocktail hour. After experiencing the afternoon tea, the Langham Club on the 22nd floor has a good environment.
